## Audio and Music

_Libraries for manipulating audio._

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;201‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;33üç¥</code></b> [flac](https://github.com/mewkiz/flac) - Native Go FLAC encoder/decoder with support for FLAC streams.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;95‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;16üç¥</code></b> [gaad](https://github.com/Comcast/gaad) - Native Go AAC bitstream parser.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;214‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;17üç¥</code></b> [GoAudio](https://github.com/DylanMeeus/GoAudio) - Native Go Audio Processing Library.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;17‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;10üç¥</code></b> [gosamplerate](https://github.com/dh1tw/gosamplerate) - libsamplerate bindings for go.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;237‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;36üç¥</code></b> [id3v2](https://github.com/bogem/id3v2) - ID3 decoding and encoding library for Go.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;167‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;32üç¥</code></b> [malgo](https://github.com/gen2brain/malgo) - Mini audio library.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;75‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;13üç¥</code></b> [minimp3](https://github.com/tosone/minimp3) - Lightweight MP3 decoder library.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;151‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;23üç¥</code></b> [mix](https://github.com/go-mix/mix) - Sequence-based Go-native audio mixer for music apps.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;383‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;40üç¥</code></b> [music-theory](https://github.com/go-music-theory/music-theory) - Music theory models in Go.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;963‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;84üç¥</code></b> [Oto](https://github.com/hajimehoshi/oto) - A low-level library to play sound on multiple platforms.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;493‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;76üç¥</code></b> [PortAudio](https://github.com/gordonklaus/portaudio) - Go bindings for the PortAudio audio I/O library.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;265‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;53üç¥</code></b> [portmidi](https://github.com/rakyll/portmidi) - Go bindings for PortMidi.

## Authentication and OAuth

_Libraries for implementing authentications schemes._

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;3006‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;184üç¥</code></b> [authboss](https://github.com/volatiletech/authboss) - Modular authentication system for the web. It tries to remove as much boilerplate and "hard things" as possible so that each time you start a new web project in Go, you can plug it in, configure, and start building your app without having to build an authentication system each time.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;29‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [branca](https://github.com/essentialkaos/branca) - branca token <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;177‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6üç¥</code></b> [specification implementation](https://github.com/tuupola/branca-spec) for Golang 1.15+.
- <b><code>&nbsp;11430‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1264üç¥</code></b> [casbin](https://github.com/hsluoyz/casbin) - Authorization library that supports access control models like ACL, RBAC, ABAC.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;11‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [cookiestxt](https://github.com/mengzhuo/cookiestxt) - provides parser of cookies.txt file format.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;40‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4üç¥</code></b> [go-email-normalizer](https://github.com/dimuska139/go-email-normalizer) - Golang library for providing a canonical representation of email address.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;346‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;35üç¥</code></b> [go-guardian](https://github.com/shaj13/go-guardian) - Go-Guardian is a golang library that provides a simple, clean, and idiomatic way to create powerful modern API and web authentication that supports LDAP, Basic, Bearer token and Certificate based authentication.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1892‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;338üç¥</code></b> [go-jose](https://github.com/square/go-jose) - Fairly complete implementation of the JOSE working group's JSON Web Token, JSON Web Signatures, and JSON Web Encryption specs.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1491‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;120üç¥</code></b> [gologin](https://github.com/dghubble/gologin) - chainable handlers for login with OAuth1 and OAuth2 authentication providers.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1251‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;155üç¥</code></b> [gorbac](https://github.com/mikespook/gorbac) - provides a lightweight role-based access control (RBAC) implementation in Golang.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;3535‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;436üç¥</code></b> [goth](https://github.com/markbates/goth) - provides a simple, clean, and idiomatic way to use OAuth and OAuth2. Handles multiple providers out of the box.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;237‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;15üç¥</code></b> [jeff](https://github.com/abraithwaite/jeff) - Simple, flexible, secure and idiomatic web session management with pluggable backends.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;281‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;21üç¥</code></b> [jwt](https://github.com/pascaldekloe/jwt) - Lightweight JSON Web Token (JWT) library.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;321‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;29üç¥</code></b> [jwt](https://github.com/cristalhq/jwt) - Safe, simple and fast JSON Web Tokens for Go.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;213‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;41üç¥</code></b> [jwt-auth](https://github.com/adam-hanna/jwt-auth) - JWT middleware for Golang http servers with many configuration options.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1846‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;161üç¥</code></b> [loginsrv](https://github.com/tarent/loginsrv) - JWT login microservice with plugable backends such as OAuth2 (Github), htpasswd, osiam.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;4046‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;823üç¥</code></b> [oauth2](https://github.com/golang/oauth2) - Successor of goauth2. Generic OAuth 2.0 package that comes with JWT, Google APIs, Compute Engine and App Engine support.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1716‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;388üç¥</code></b> [osin](https://github.com/openshift/osin) - Golang OAuth2 server library.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;116‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8üç¥</code></b> [otpgen](https://github.com/grijul/otpgen) - Library to generate TOTP/HOTP codes.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;27‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [otpgo](https://github.com/jltorresm/otpgo) - Time-Based One-Time Password (TOTP) and HMAC-Based One-Time Password (HOTP) library for Go.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;579‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;29üç¥</code></b> [paseto](https://github.com/o1egl/paseto) - Golang implementation of Platform-Agnostic Security Tokens (PASETO).
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;446‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;37üç¥</code></b> [permissions2](https://github.com/xyproto/permissions2) - Library for keeping track of users, login states and permissions. Uses secure cookies and bcrypt.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;90‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;16üç¥</code></b> [rbac](https://github.com/zpatrick/rbac) - Minimalistic RBAC package for Go applications.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;19‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6üç¥</code></b> [scope](https://github.com/SonicRoshan/scope) - Easily Manage OAuth2 Scopes In Go.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1056‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;99üç¥</code></b> [scs](https://github.com/alexedwards/scs) - Session Manager for HTTP servers.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;55‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9üç¥</code></b> [securecookie](https://github.com/chmike/securecookie) - Efficient secure cookie encoding/decoding.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;107‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;18üç¥</code></b> [session](https://github.com/icza/session) - Go session management for web servers (including support for Google App Engine - GAE).
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;10‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2üç¥</code></b> [sessiongate-go](https://github.com/f0rmiga/sessiongate-go) - Go session management using the SessionGate Redis module.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;62‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9üç¥</code></b> [sessions](https://github.com/adam-hanna/sessions) - Dead simple, highly performant, highly customizable sessions service for go http servers.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;114‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7üç¥</code></b> [sessionup](https://github.com/swithek/sessionup) - Simple, yet effective HTTP session management and identification package.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;97‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9üç¥</code></b> [sjwt](https://github.com/brianvoe/sjwt) - Simple jwt generator and parser.

## Blockchain

_Tools for building blockchains._

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;3488‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1544üç¥</code></b> [cosmos-sdk](https://github.com/cosmos/cosmos-sdk) - A Framework for Building Public Blockchains in the Cosmos Ecosystem.
- <b><code>&nbsp;35907‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;13317üç¥</code></b> [go-ethereum](https://github.com/ethereum/go-ethereum) - Official Go implementation of the Ethereum protocol.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;306‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;81üç¥</code></b> [gossamer](https://github.com/ChainSafe/gossamer) - A Go implementation of the Polkadot Host.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;224‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;43üç¥</code></b> [solana-go](https://github.com/gagliardetto/solana-go) - Go library to interface with Solana JSON RPC and WebSocket interfaces.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;4698‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1542üç¥</code></b> [tendermint](https://github.com/tendermint/tendermint) - High-performance middleware for transforming a state machine written in any programming language into a Byzantine Fault Tolerant replicated state machine using the Tendermint consensus and blockchain protocols.

## Bot Building

_Libraries for building and working with bots._

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;78‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9üç¥</code></b> [echotron](https://github.com/NicoNex/echotron) - An elegant and concurrent library for Telegram Bots in Go.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;57‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9üç¥</code></b> [ephemeral-roles](https://github.com/ewohltman/ephemeral-roles) - A Discord bot for managing ephemeral roles based upon voice channel member presence.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;722‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;177üç¥</code></b> [go-chat-bot](https://github.com/go-chat-bot/bot) - IRC, Slack & Telegram bot written in Go.
- üåé [go-joe](https://joe-bot.net) - A general-purpose bot library inspired by Hubot but written in Go.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;218‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;16üç¥</code></b> [go-sarah](https://github.com/oklahomer/go-sarah) - Framework to build bot for desired chat services including LINE, Slack, Gitter and more.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;112‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [go-tgbot](https://github.com/olebedev/go-tgbot) - Pure Golang Telegram Bot API wrapper, generated from swagger file, session-based router and middleware.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;218‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;48üç¥</code></b> [go-twitch-irc](https://github.com/gempir/go-twitch-irc) - Library to write bots for twitch.tv chat
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;715‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;190üç¥</code></b> [Golang CryptoTrading Bot](https://github.com/saniales/golang-crypto-trading-bot) - A golang implementation of a console-based trading bot for cryptocurrency exchanges.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;38‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4üç¥</code></b> [govkbot](https://github.com/nikepan/govkbot) - Simple Go üåé [VK](https://vk.com) bot library.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;136‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;24üç¥</code></b> [hanu](https://github.com/sbstjn/hanu) - Framework for writing Slack bots.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;857‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;202üç¥</code></b> [Kelp](https://github.com/stellar/kelp) - official trading and market-making bot for the üåé [Stellar](https://www.stellar.org/) DEX. Works out-of-the-box, written in Golang, compatible with centralized exchanges and custom trading strategies.

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;66‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;10üç¥</code></b> [bloom](https://github.com/yourbasic/bloom) - Golang Bloom filter implementation.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2üç¥</code></b> [bloomfilter](https://github.com/OldPanda/bloomfilter) - Yet another Bloomfilter implementation in Go, compatible with Java's Guava library.

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;23‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [cmap](https://github.com/lrita/cmap) - a thread-safe concurrent map for go, support using `interface{}` as key and auto scale up shards.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;39‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8üç¥</code></b> [concurrent-writer](https://github.com/free/concurrent-writer) - Highly concurrent drop-in replacement for `bufio.Writer`.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;103‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;14üç¥</code></b> [conjungo](https://github.com/InVisionApp/conjungo) - A small, powerful and flexible merge library.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;55‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [count-min-log](https://github.com/seiflotfy/count-min-log) - Go implementation Count-Min-Log sketch: Approximately counting with approximate counters (Like Count-Min sketch but using less memory).
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;51‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8üç¥</code></b> [crunch](https://github.com/superwhiskers/crunch) - Go package implementing buffers for handling various datatypes easily.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;200‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;18üç¥</code></b> [cuckoo-filter](https://github.com/linvon/cuckoo-filter) - Cuckoo filter: a comprehensive cuckoo filter, which is configurable and space optimized compared with other implements, and all features mentioned in original paper is available.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;886‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;80üç¥</code></b> [cuckoofilter](https://github.com/seiflotfy/cuckoofilter) - Cuckoo filter: a good alternative to a counting bloom filter implemented in Go.

## Database

_Databases implemented in Go._

- <b><code>&nbsp;10505‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;932üç¥</code></b> [badger](https://github.com/dgraph-io/badger) - Fast key-value store in Go.

- üåé [Bitcask](https://git.mills.io/prologic/bitcask) - Bitcask is an embeddable, persistent and fast key-value (KV) database written in pure Go with predictable read/write performance, low latency and high throughput thanks to the bitcask on-disk layout (LSM+WAL).
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;3662‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;259üç¥</code></b> [buntdb](https://github.com/tidwall/buntdb) - Fast, embeddable, in-memory key/value database for Go with custom indexing and spatial support.

## Database Drivers

_Libraries for connecting and operating databases._

- Relational Databases
  - <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;89‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;26üç¥</code></b> [avatica](https://github.com/apache/calcite-avatica-go) - Apache Avatica/Phoenix SQL driver for database/sql.
  - <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;16‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6üç¥</code></b> [bgc](https://github.com/viant/bgc) - Datastore Connectivity for BigQuery for go.
  - <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;168‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;50üç¥</code></b> [firebirdsql](https://github.com/nakagami/firebirdsql) - Firebird RDBMS SQL driver for Go.
  - <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;128‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;31üç¥</code></b> [go-adodb](https://github.com/mattn/go-adodb) - Microsoft ActiveX Object DataBase driver for go that uses database/sql.
  - <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1529‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;398üç¥</code></b> [go-mssqldb](https://github.com/denisenkom/go-mssqldb) - Microsoft MSSQL driver for Go.
  - <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;579‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;209üç¥</code></b> [go-oci8](https://github.com/mattn/go-oci8) - Oracle driver for go that uses database/sql.
  - <b><code>&nbsp;11944‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2083üç¥</code></b> [go-sql-driver/mysql](https://github.com/go-sql-driver/mysql) - MySQL driver for Go.
  - <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;5489‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;915üç¥</code></b> [go-sqlite3](https://github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3) - SQLite3 driver for go that uses database/sql.
  - <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;336‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;72üç¥</code></b> [godror](https://github.com/godror/godror) - Oracle driver for Go, using the ODPI-C driver.
  - <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;106‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;45üç¥</code></b> [gofreetds](https://github.com/minus5/gofreetds) - Microsoft MSSQL driver. Go wrapper over üåé [FreeTDS](https://www.freetds.org).
  - <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;5127‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;502üç¥</code></b> [pgx](https://github.com/jackc/pgx) - PostgreSQL driver supporting features beyond those exposed by database/sql.
  - <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2üç¥</code></b> [pig](https://github.com/alexeyco/pig) - Simple <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;5127‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;502üç¥</code></b> [pgx](https://github.com/jackc/pgx) wrapper to execute and <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;509‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;35üç¥</code></b> [scan](https://github.com/georgysavva/scany) query results easily.
  - <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;7121‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;844üç¥</code></b> [pq](https://github.com/lib/pq) - Pure Go Postgres driver for database/sql.
  - <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;105‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;11üç¥</code></b> [Sqinn-Go](https://github.com/cvilsmeier/sqinn-go) - SQLite with pure Go.
  - <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;522‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;35üç¥</code></b> [sqlhooks](https://github.com/qustavo/sqlhooks) - Attach hooks to any database/sql driver.

- NoSQL Databases
  - <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;382‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;176üç¥</code></b> [aerospike-client-go](https://github.com/aerospike/aerospike-client-go) - Aerospike client in Go language.

  - <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;313‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;91üç¥</code></b> [go-couchbase](https://github.com/couchbase/go-couchbase) - Couchbase client in Go.
  - <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;51‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;23üç¥</code></b> [go-pilosa](https://github.com/pilosa/go-pilosa) - Go client library for Pilosa.
  - <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;253‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;40üç¥</code></b> [go-rejson](https://github.com/nitishm/go-rejson) - Golang client for redislabs' ReJSON module using Redigo golang client. Store and manipulate structs as JSON objects in redis with ease.
  - <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;332‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;96üç¥</code></b> [gocb](https://github.com/couchbase/gocb) - Official Couchbase Go SDK.
  - <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [gocosmos](https://github.com/btnguyen2k/gocosmos) - REST client and standard `database/sql` driver for Azure Cosmos DB.

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;128‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9üç¥</code></b> [artifex](https://github.com/borderstech/artifex) - Simple in-memory job queue for Golang using worker-based dispatching.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;39‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [async](https://github.com/reugn/async) - An alternative sync library for Go (Future, Promise, Locks).
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;102‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;14üç¥</code></b> [async](https://github.com/studiosol/async) - A safe way to execute functions asynchronously, recovering them in case of panic.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1üç¥</code></b> [breaker](https://github.com/kamilsk/breaker) - Flexible mechanism to make execution flow interruptible.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;18‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2üç¥</code></b> [channelify](https://github.com/ddelizia/channelify) - Transform your function to return channels for easy and powerful parallel processing.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [concurrency-limiter](https://github.com/vivek-ng/concurrency-limiter) - Concurrency limiter with support for timeouts , dynamic priority and context cancellation of goroutines.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;12‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2üç¥</code></b> [conexec](https://github.com/ITcathyh/conexec) - A concurrent toolkit to help execute funcs concurrently in an efficient and safe way. It supports specifying the overall timeout to avoid blocking and uses goroutine pool to improve efficiency.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;93‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;13üç¥</code></b> [cyclicbarrier](https://github.com/marusama/cyclicbarrier) - CyclicBarrier for golang.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;10‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2üç¥</code></b> [execpool](https://github.com/hexdigest/execpool) - A pool built around exec.Cmd that spins up a given number of processes in advance and attaches stdin and stdout to them when needed. Very similar to FastCGI or Apache Prefork MPM but works for any command.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;227‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;18üç¥</code></b> [go-floc](https://github.com/workanator/go-floc) - Orchestrate goroutines with ease.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;186‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;21üç¥</code></b> [go-flow](https://github.com/kamildrazkiewicz/go-flow) - Control goroutines execution order.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [go-tools/multithreading](https://github.com/nikhilsaraf/go-tools) - Manage a pool of goroutines using this lightweight library with a simple API.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;25‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8üç¥</code></b> [go-trylock](https://github.com/subchen/go-trylock) - TryLock support on read-write lock for Golang.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;29‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2üç¥</code></b> [go-waitgroup](https://github.com/pieterclaerhout/go-waitgroup) - Like `sync.WaitGroup` with error handling and concurrency control.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;136‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;11üç¥</code></b> [go-workers](https://github.com/catmullet/go-workers) - Easily and safely run workers for large data processing pipelines.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;46‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7üç¥</code></b> [goccm](https://github.com/zenthangplus/goccm) - Go Concurrency Manager package limits the number of goroutines that allowed to run concurrently.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;32‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4üç¥</code></b> [gohive](https://github.com/loveleshsharma/gohive) - A highly performant and easy to use Goroutine pool for Go.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;77‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9üç¥</code></b> [gollback](https://github.com/vardius/gollback) - asynchronous simple function utilities, for managing execution of closures and callbacks.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;14‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [gowl](https://github.com/hamed-yousefi/gowl) - Gowl is a process management and process monitoring tool at once. An infinite worker pool gives you the ability to control the pool and processes and monitor their status.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2636‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;243üç¥</code></b> [goworker](https://github.com/benmanns/goworker) - goworker is a Go-based background worker.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;364‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;60üç¥</code></b> [gowp](https://github.com/xxjwxc/gowp) - gowp is concurrency limiting goroutine pool.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;84‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [gpool](https://github.com/Sherifabdlnaby/gpool) - manages a resizeable pool of context-aware goroutines to bound concurrency.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;676‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;98üç¥</code></b> [grpool](https://github.com/ivpusic/grpool) - Lightweight Goroutine pool.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [hands](https://github.com/duanckham/hands) - A process controller used to control the execution and return strategies of multiple goroutines.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;74‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8üç¥</code></b> [Hunch](https://github.com/AaronJan/Hunch) - Hunch provides functions like: `All`, `First`, `Retry`, `Waterfall` etc., that makes asynchronous flow control more intuitive.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;37‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2üç¥</code></b> [kyoo](https://github.com/dirkaholic/kyoo) - Provides an unlimited job queue and concurrent worker pools.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;111‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8üç¥</code></b> [neilotoole/errgroup](https://github.com/neilotoole/errgroup) - Drop-in alternative to `sync/errgroup`, limited to a pool of N worker goroutines.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;40‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [nursery](https://github.com/arunsworld/nursery) - Structured concurrency in Go.
- üåé [oversight](https://cirello.io/oversight) - Oversight is a complete implementation of the Erlang supervision trees.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;33‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2üç¥</code></b> [parallel-fn](https://github.com/rafaeljesus/parallel-fn) - Run functions in parallel.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;467‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;32üç¥</code></b> [pond](https://github.com/alitto/pond) - Minimalistic and High-performance goroutine worker pool written in Go.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;672‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;60üç¥</code></b> [pool](https://github.com/go-playground/pool) - Limited consumer goroutine or unlimited goroutine pool for easier goroutine handling and cancellation.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;12‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2üç¥</code></b> [queue](https://github.com/AnikHasibul/queue) - Gives you a `sync.WaitGroup` like queue group accessibility. Helps you to throttle and limit goroutines, wait for the end of the all goroutines and much more.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;48‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7üç¥</code></b> [routine](https://github.com/x-mod/routine) - go routine control with context, support: Main, Go, Pool and some useful Executors.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;90‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;12üç¥</code></b> [semaphore](https://github.com/kamilsk/semaphore) - Semaphore pattern implementation with timeout of lock/unlock operations based on channel and context.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;140‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9üç¥</code></b> [semaphore](https://github.com/marusama/semaphore) - Fast resizable semaphore implementation based on CAS (faster than channel-based semaphore implementations).
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;23‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4üç¥</code></b> [stl](https://github.com/ssgreg/stl) - Software transactional locks based on Software Transactional Memory (STM) concurrency control mechanism.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;69‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;15üç¥</code></b> [threadpool](https://github.com/shettyh/threadpool) - Golang threadpool implementation.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2896‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;252üç¥</code></b> [tunny](https://github.com/Jeffail/tunny) - Goroutine pool for golang.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;82‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;14üç¥</code></b> [worker-pool](https://github.com/vardius/worker-pool) - goworker is a Go simple async worker pool.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;740‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;96üç¥</code></b> [workerpool](https://github.com/gammazero/workerpool) - Goroutine pool that limits the concurrency of task execution, not the number of tasks queued.

## Job Scheduler

_Libraries for scheduling jobs._

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;22‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [cheek](https://github.com/datarootsio/cheek) - A simple crontab like scheduler that aims to offer a KISS approach to job scheduling.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;116‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;13üç¥</code></b> [clockwerk](https://github.com/onatm/clockwerk) - Go package to schedule periodic jobs using a simple, fluent syntax.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [cronticker](https://github.com/krayzpipes/cronticker) - A ticker implementation to support cron schedules.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;209‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;18üç¥</code></b> [go-cron](https://github.com/rk/go-cron) - Simple Cron library for go that can execute closures or functions at varying intervals, from once a second to once a year on a specific date and time. Primarily for web applications and long running daemons.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;596‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;38üç¥</code></b> [go-quartz](https://github.com/reugn/go-quartz) - Simple, zero-dependency scheduling library for Go.

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;14‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1üç¥</code></b> [goflow](https://github.com/fieldryand/goflow) - A workflow orchestrator and scheduler for rapid prototyping of ETL/ML/AI pipelines.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;884‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;55üç¥</code></b> [gron](https://github.com/roylee0704/gron) - Define time-based tasks using a simple Go API and Gron‚Äôs scheduler will run them accordingly.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;182‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;13üç¥</code></b> [gronx](https://github.com/adhocore/gronx) - Cron expression parser, task runner and daemon consuming crontab like task list.

Works in combination with encoding/json and other packages that "Unmarshal" arbitrary data into Go data-types.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;10‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [dynjson](https://github.com/cocoonspace/dynjson) - Client-customizable JSON formats for dynamic APIs.

## ORM

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;18‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1üç¥</code></b> [cacheme](https://github.com/Yiling-J/cacheme-go) - Schema based, typed Redis caching/memoize framework for Go.

- <b><code>&nbsp;27076‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;3073üç¥</code></b> [GORM](https://github.com/go-gorm/gorm) - The fantastic ORM library for Golang, aims to be developer friendly.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1731‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;282üç¥</code></b> [gormt](https://github.com/xxjwxc/gormt) - Mysql database to golang gorm struct.

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;10‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [lore](https://github.com/abrahambotros/lore) - Simple and lightweight pseudo-ORM/pseudo-struct-mapping environment for Go.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;11‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [marlow](https://github.com/marlow/marlow) - Generated ORM from project structs for compile time safety assurances.

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1163‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;62üç¥</code></b> [Prisma](https://github.com/prisma/prisma-client-go) - Prisma Client Go, Typesafe database access for Go.

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2904‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;207üç¥</code></b> [upper.io/db](https://github.com/upper/db) - Single interface for interacting with different data sources through the use of adapters that wrap mature database drivers.
- üåé [XORM](https://gitea.com/xorm/xorm) - Simple and powerful ORM for Go. (Support: MySQL, MyMysql, PostgreSQL, Tidb, SQLite3, MsSql and Oracle).
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;287‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;27üç¥</code></b> [Zoom](https://github.com/albrow/zoom) - Blazing-fast datastore and querying engine built on Redis.

## Package Management

_Official tooling for dependency and package management_

- üåé [go modules](https://golang.org/cmd/go/#hdr-Modules__module_versions__and_more) - Modules are the unit of source code interchange and versioning. The go command has direct support for working with modules, including recording and resolving dependencies on other modules.

_Official experimental tooling for package management_

- <b><code>&nbsp;13071‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1109üç¥</code></b> [dep](https://github.com/golang/dep) - Go dependency tool.
- üåé [vgo](https://go.googlesource.com/vgo/) - Versioned Go.

_Unofficial libraries for package and dependency management._

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;8152‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;548üç¥</code></b> [glide](https://github.com/Masterminds/glide) - Manage your golang vendor and vendored packages with ease. Inspired by tools like Maven, Bundler, and Pip.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;5599‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;483üç¥</code></b> [godep](https://github.com/tools/godep) - dependency tool for go, godep helps build packages reproducibly by fixing their dependencies.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1398‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;104üç¥</code></b> [gom](https://github.com/mattn/gom) - Go Manager - bundle for go.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;779‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;45üç¥</code></b> [goop](https://github.com/nitrous-io/goop) - Simple dependency manager for Go (golang), inspired by Bundler.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;48‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6üç¥</code></b> [gop](https://github.com/lunny/gop) - Build and manage your Go applications out of GOPATH.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2490‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;219üç¥</code></b> [gopm](https://github.com/gpmgo/gopm) - Go Package Manager.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;4985‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;413üç¥</code></b> [govendor](https://github.com/kardianos/govendor) - Go Package Manager. Go vendor tool that works with the standard vendor file.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1200‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;51üç¥</code></b> [gpm](https://github.com/pote/gpm) - Barebones dependency manager for Go.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;213‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7üç¥</code></b> [johnny-deps](https://github.com/VividCortex/johnny-deps) - Minimal dependency version using Git.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;399‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;14üç¥</code></b> [modgv](https://github.com/lucasepe/modgv) - Converts 'go mod graph' output into Graphviz's DOT language.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;133‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;28üç¥</code></b> [mvn-golang](https://github.com/raydac/mvn-golang) - plugin that provides way for auto-loading of Golang SDK, dependency management and start build environment in Maven project infrastructure.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;237‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;11üç¥</code></b> [nut](https://github.com/jingweno/nut) - Vendor Go dependencies.

## Security

_Libraries that are used to help make your application more secure._

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1895‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;129üç¥</code></b> [acmetool](https://github.com/hlandau/acme) - ACME (Let's Encrypt) client tool with automatic renewal.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;948‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;102üç¥</code></b> [acra](https://github.com/cossacklabs/acra) - Network encryption proxy to protect database-based applications from data leaks: strong selective encryption, SQL injections prevention, intrusion detection system.
- <b><code>&nbsp;10070‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;319üç¥</code></b> [age](https://github.com/FiloSottile/age) - A simple, modern and secure encryption tool (and Go library) with small explicit keys, no config options, and UNIX-style composability.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;16‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [argon2-hashing](https://github.com/andskur/argon2-hashing) - light wrapper around Go's argon2 package that closely mirrors with Go's standard library Bcrypt and simple-scrypt package.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;89‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;10üç¥</code></b> [argon2pw](https://github.com/raja/argon2pw) - Argon2 password hash generation with constant-time password comparison.
- üåé [autocert](https://godoc.org/golang.org/x/crypto/acme/autocert) - Auto provision Let's Encrypt certificates and start a TLS server.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;305‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;17üç¥</code></b> [BadActor](https://github.com/jaredfolkins/badactor) - In-memory, application-driven jailer built in the spirit of fail2ban.

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;23‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6üç¥</code></b> [certificates](https://github.com/mvmaasakkers/certificates) - An opinionated tool for generating tls certificates.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;3941‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;207üç¥</code></b> [CertMagic](https://github.com/caddyserver/certmagic) - Mature, robust, and powerful ACME client integration for fully-managed TLS certificate issuance and renewal.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;73‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6üç¥</code></b> [dongle](https://github.com/golang-module/dongle) - A simple, semantic and developer-friendly golang package for encoding&decoding and encryption&decryption.

  - <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;74‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8üç¥</code></b> [align](https://github.com/Guitarbum722/align) - A general purpose application that aligns text.

## UUID

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;14‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [uuid](https://github.com/agext/uuid) - Generate, encode, and decode UUIDs v1 with fast or cryptographic-quality random node identifier.

### Middlewares

#### Actual middlewares

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;19‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6üç¥</code></b> [client-timing](https://github.com/posener/client-timing) - An HTTP client for Server-Timing header.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2028‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;188üç¥</code></b> [CORS](https://github.com/rs/cors) - Easily add CORS capabilities to your API.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;36‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [formjson](https://github.com/rs/formjson) - Transparently handle JSON input as a standard form POST.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;420‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;21üç¥</code></b> [go-fault](https://github.com/github/go-fault) - Fault injection middleware for Go.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;830‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;31üç¥</code></b> [go-server-timing](https://github.com/mitchellh/go-server-timing) - Add/parse Server-Timing header.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1512‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;114üç¥</code></b> [Limiter](https://github.com/ulule/limiter) - Dead simple rate limit middleware for Go.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;120‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9üç¥</code></b> [ln-paywall](https://github.com/philippgille/ln-paywall) - Go middleware for monetizing APIs on a per-request basis with the Lightning Network (Bitcoin).
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1üç¥</code></b> [mid](https://github.com/bobg/mid) - Miscellaneous HTTP middleware features: idiomatic error return from handlers; receive/respond with JSON data; request tracing; and more.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;26‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [rk-gin](https://github.com/rookie-ninja/rk-gin) - Middleware for Gin framework with logging, metrics, auth, tracing etc.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;26‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [rk-grpc](https://github.com/rookie-ninja/rk-grpc) - Middleware for gRPC with logging, metrics, auth, tracing etc.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2120‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;193üç¥</code></b> [Tollbooth](https://github.com/didip/tollbooth) - Rate limit HTTP request handler.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;89‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;22üç¥</code></b> [XFF](https://github.com/sebest/xff) - Handle `X-Forwarded-For` header and friends.

#### Libraries for creating HTTP middlewares

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2498‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;139üç¥</code></b> [alice](https://github.com/justinas/alice) - Painless middleware chaining for Go.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2üç¥</code></b> [catena](https://github.com/codemodus/catena) - http.Handler wrapper catenation (same API as "chain").
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;64‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [chain](https://github.com/codemodus/chain) - Handler wrapper chaining with scoped data (net/context-based "middleware").
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;60‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6üç¥</code></b> [go-wrap](https://github.com/go-on/wrap) - Small middlewares package for net/http.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;98‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4üç¥</code></b> [gores](https://github.com/alioygur/gores) - Go package that handles HTML, JSON, XML and etc. responses. Useful for RESTful APIs.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;296‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;17üç¥</code></b> [interpose](https://github.com/carbocation/interpose) - Minimalist net/http middleware for golang.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;78‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7üç¥</code></b> [mediary](https://github.com/HereMobilityDevelopers/mediary) - add interceptors to `http.Client` to allow dumping/shaping/tracing/... of requests/responses.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;210‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;15üç¥</code></b> [muxchain](https://github.com/stephens2424/muxchain) - Lightweight middleware for net/http.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;7154‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;577üç¥</code></b> [negroni](https://github.com/urfave/negroni) - Idiomatic HTTP middleware for Golang.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1580‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;129üç¥</code></b> [render](https://github.com/unrolled/render) - Go package for easily rendering JSON, XML, and HTML template responses.

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;97‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;14üç¥</code></b> [rye](https://github.com/InVisionApp/rye) - Tiny Go middleware library (with canned Middlewares) that supports JWT, CORS, Statsd, and Go 1.7 context.

### Routers

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;121‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;12üç¥</code></b> [alien](https://github.com/gernest/alien) - Lightweight and fast http router from outer space.

It works with routes of varying difficulty, length and nesting. And he knows how to create a URL from the received parameters.

## Benchmarks

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;92‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;28üç¥</code></b> [autobench](https://github.com/davecheney/autobench) - Framework to compare the performance between different Go versions.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;22‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [go-benchmark-app](https://github.com/mrLSD/go-benchmark-app) - Powerful HTTP-benchmark tool mixed with –êb, Wrk, Siege tools. Gathering statistics and various parameters for benchmarks and comparison results.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;143‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;26üç¥</code></b> [go-benchmarks](https://github.com/tylertreat/go-benchmarks) - Few miscellaneous Go microbenchmarks. Compare some language features to alternative approaches.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1543‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;217üç¥</code></b> [go-http-routing-benchmark](https://github.com/julienschmidt/go-http-routing-benchmark) - Go HTTP request router benchmark and comparison.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1üç¥</code></b> [go-json-benchmark](https://github.com/zerosnake0/go-json-benchmark) - Go JSON benchmark.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;21‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1üç¥</code></b> [go-ml-benchmarks](https://github.com/nikolaydubina/go-ml-benchmarks) - benchmarks for machine learning inference in Go.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1644‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;184üç¥</code></b> [go-web-framework-benchmark](https://github.com/smallnest/go-web-framework-benchmark) - Go web framework benchmark.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1258‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;127üç¥</code></b> [go_serialization_benchmarks](https://github.com/alecthomas/go_serialization_benchmarks) - Benchmarks of Go serialization methods.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;57‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [gocostmodel](https://github.com/PuerkitoBio/gocostmodel) - Benchmarks of common basic operations for the Go language.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;61‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;14üç¥</code></b> [golang-sql-benchmark](https://github.com/tyler-smith/golang-sql-benchmark) - Collection of benchmarks for popular Go database/SQL utilities.

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;24‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2üç¥</code></b> [kvbench](https://github.com/jimrobinson/kvbench) - Key/Value database benchmark.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1006‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;131üç¥</code></b> [skynet](https://github.com/atemerev/skynet) - Skynet 1M threads microbenchmark.
